## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What are PHP Cookies?**  

‚úÖ **PHP Cookies** ‡¶π‡¶≤ **small pieces of data** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **user's browser-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **server-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶£** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  

‚úÖ **Cookies ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü:**  
- **User Authentication** ‚Äì User login state store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  
- **Preferences Management** ‚Äì Theme, Language, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Settings ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  
- **Shopping Cart Management** ‚Äì E-commerce ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá **cart items** ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use Cookies?**  

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **User Identification** | Logged-in user ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **Personalized Content** | User-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ content ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |
| **Shopping Cart** | Products ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |
| **Session Tracking** | User ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶ø track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ |

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **Creating Cookies in PHP**  

üîπ **PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Cookies ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `setcookie()` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Syntax:**  
```php
setcookie(name, value, expire, path, domain, secure, httponly);
```
| Parameter | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| **name** | Cookie-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ |
| **value** | Cookie-‡¶è‡¶∞ value |
| **expire** | ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá cookie expire ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá (UNIX timestamp) |
| **path** | Cookie **‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® directory/subdirectory** ‡¶§‡ßá valid ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá |
| **domain** | Cookie **‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® domain** ‡¶è valid ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá |
| **secure** | `true` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá cookie **HTTPS ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá** |
| **httponly** | `true` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá cookie **JavaScript ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ** |

‚úÖ **Example: Creating a Cookie**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("username", "JohnDoe", time() + 3600, "/"); // 1 Hour Expiry
echo "Cookie has been set!";
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- `"username"` ‚Üí Cookie-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§  
- `"JohnDoe"` ‚Üí Cookie-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§  
- `time() + 3600` ‚Üí 1 ‡¶ò‡¶£‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Cookie ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§  
- `"/"` ‚Üí ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã website ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡ßú‡ßá cookie valid ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§  

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Retrieving Cookies in PHP**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá `$_COOKIE` Superglobal ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Cookies ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Get a Cookie**  
```php
<?php
if (isset($_COOKIE["username"])) {
    echo "Welcome, " . $_COOKIE["username"];
} else {
    echo "No cookie found!";
}
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- `isset($_COOKIE["username"])` ‚Üí ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Cookie ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
- **If available**, Cookie-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® print ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Updating Cookies in PHP**  

üîπ **Cookies Update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶π `setcookie()` ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Updating a Cookie**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("username", "Alice", time() + 3600, "/");
echo "Cookie has been updated!";
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßã **"JohnDoe"** cookie **‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® "Alice" ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§  

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Deleting Cookies in PHP**  

üîπ **Cookies ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡¶§‡ßá, `setcookie()` ‡¶ï‡ßá `time() - 3600` (Past Time) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Deleting a Cookie**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("username", "", time() - 3600, "/");
echo "Cookie has been deleted!";
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- `time() - 3600` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Cookie **‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ò‡¶£‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü**, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá Cookie ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Setting Expiration Time for Cookies**  

‚úÖ **Example: Expiring Cookie After 1 Day**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("user_pref", "dark_mode", time() + (86400 * 1), "/"); // 1 day
?>
```
‚úÖ **Example: Expiring Cookie After 1 Year**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("theme", "light", time() + (86400 * 365), "/"); // 1 Year
?>
```

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Secure Cookie Handling**  

üîπ **Security Risks Prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `secure` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `httponly` Flags ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Secure HTTP-only Cookie**  
```php
<?php
setcookie("auth_token", "randomtoken123", time() + 3600, "/", "", true, true);
?>
```
| Parameter | Explanation |
|-----------|-------------|
| `true` (Secure) | Cookie ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ **HTTPS ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá**‡•§ |
| `true` (HttpOnly) | Cookie **JavaScript ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ (XSS Protection)**‡•§ |

---

## **üîç HTTP ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTTPS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ**

## **1Ô∏è‚É£ HTTP (HyperText Transfer Protocol)**
**HTTP** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶≤**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü (‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ (‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®-‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶°** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

üîπ **‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá HTTP ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?**
- ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ **‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º (Request)‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º (Response)‡•§
- ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

üîπ **HTTP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø**
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **Unsecure** (‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§)‡•§
- ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ **Encryption ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ** ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **MITM (Man-in-the-Middle Attack)** ‡¶ù‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- URL ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º **`http://`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§

üîπ **HTTP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£**
```
http://www.example.com
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **HTTP** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **unencrypted** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **less secure**‡•§

---

## **2Ô∏è‚É£ HTTPS (HyperText Transfer Protocol Secure)**
**HTTPS** ‡¶π‡¶≤ **HTTP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ (Secure) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£**, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **SSL/TLS (Secure Sockets Layer / Transport Layer Security) Encryption** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

üîπ **HTTPS ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?**
- ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **SSL/TLS Encryption** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ **encrypted** ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá**, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

üîπ **HTTPS-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø**
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **Secure** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Encrypted**‡•§
- ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ **‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶®**‡•§
- **SSL/TLS ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ü** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§
- URL ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º **`https://`** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§
- **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ üîí ‡¶Ü‡¶á‡¶ï‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**‡•§

üîπ **HTTPS-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£**
```
https://www.example.com
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **HTTPS** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **encrypted** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **safe for sensitive data**‡•§

---

## **üîÑ HTTP ‡¶¨‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ HTTPS ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£**

| ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø | HTTP | HTTPS |
|-----------|------|-------|
| **Security (‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ)** | ‚ùå ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶®‡ßü | ‚úÖ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ (SSL/TLS Encryption) |
| **Data Encryption** | ‚ùå ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á | ‚úÖ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá |
| **Data Integrity** | ‚ùå ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ | ‚úÖ ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ |
| **SEO Ranking** | ‚ùå ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü | ‚úÖ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü |
| **Usage (‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞)** | ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü | ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç, ‡¶á-‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏, ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü |

---

## **üîê ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® HTTPS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡ßé?**
‚úÖ **Security (‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ):** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  
‚úÖ **SEO Ranking:** ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡¶≤ HTTPS ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§  
‚úÖ **User Trust:** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ üîí ‡¶Ü‡¶á‡¶ï‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  
‚úÖ **Data Integrity:** ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‚úÖ **Online Payments:** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï ‡¶ì ‡¶á-‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§  

---

## **üåç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá HTTP ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá HTTPS-‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®?**
1Ô∏è‚É£ **SSL/TLS Certificate** ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶® (Let‚Äôs Encrypt ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü)‡•§  
2Ô∏è‚É£ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ **‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá SSL ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**‡•§  
3Ô∏è‚É£ **.htaccess** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá HTTP ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá HTTPS ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:  
```apache
RewriteEngine On
RewriteCond %{HTTPS} !=on
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}/$1 [R=301,L]
```
4Ô∏è‚É£ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ **config ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**‡•§  
5Ô∏è‚É£ **Google Search Console** ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® HTTPS URL ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§  

---

## **üîö ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞**
üîπ **HTTP** ‡¶π‡¶≤ **Unsecure Protocol**, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§  
üîπ **HTTPS** ‡¶π‡¶≤ **Secure Protocol**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **SSL/TLS Encryption** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  
üîπ **Google ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Browser** ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **HTTPS ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü**‡•§  
üîπ **‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç, ‡¶á-‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∏, ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¶‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®-‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá HTTPS ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡•§**  

## 9Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **Always Set Expiry Time for Cookies**  
```php
setcookie("user", "John", time() + 3600, "/"); // 1 Hour Expiry
```

‚úÖ **Use Secure and HttpOnly Flags**  
```php
setcookie("session_id", "xyz123", time() + 3600, "/", "", true, true);
```

‚úÖ **Check if Cookie Exists Before Accessing**  
```php
if (isset($_COOKIE["username"])) {
    echo "User: " . $_COOKIE["username"];
}
```

‚úÖ **Delete Cookies Properly**  
```php
setcookie("username", "", time() - 3600, "/");
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **Cookies** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **user preferences, authentication, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç session tracking** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ **client-side storage mechanism**‡•§  

‚úÖ **Key Features:**  
- `setcookie()` ‚Üí Cookie ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- `$_COOKIE` ‚Üí Cookie ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- `time() + EXPIRY_TIME` ‚Üí Cookie ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§  
- `time() - 3600` ‚Üí Cookie ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡•§  
- **Secure Cookies** ‚Üí `Secure` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `HttpOnly` flags ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-26: PHP Sessions

PHP **Sessions** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **server-side storage mechanism**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **multiple pages ‡¶è data persist** ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ data **server-side store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **client-side ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ**‡•§  

---

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What is a PHP Session?**  

‚úÖ **PHP Session** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **server-side storage** ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **user-specific data store** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚úÖ **Session ID** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá server **user-‡¶è‡¶∞ session track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  

üîπ **Example Use Cases:**  
- **User Authentication (Login System)**  
- **Shopping Cart Management**  
- **User Preferences Storage**  
- **Multi-page Form Handling**  

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use PHP Sessions?**  

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **Server-side Storage** | Data server ‡¶è store ‡¶π‡ßü, client-side ‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßü‡•§ |
| **More Secure than Cookies** | Data browser ‡¶è store ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á security ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø‡•§ |
| **User Tracking Possible** | ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ user ‡¶ï‡ßá track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§ |
| **Temporary Storage** | User ‡¶è‡¶∞ session-based temporary data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |

‚úÖ **Cookies vs Sessions**  

| Feature | Cookies | Sessions |
|---------|---------|----------|
| **Storage Location** | Client-side | Server-side |
| **Security** | ‡¶ï‡¶Æ | ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø |
| **Expiry** | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü | ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ user active ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ |

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **Starting a Session in PHP**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá session ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `session_start()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Start a Session**  
```php
<?php
session_start();
?>
```

üîπ **`session_start()` ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü PHP ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Full Code**  
```php
<?php
session_start(); // Start session

$_SESSION["username"] = "JohnDoe"; // Set session variable
echo "Session Started. Username is " . $_SESSION["username"];
?>
```

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Setting and Retrieving Session Variables**  

### ‚úÖ **1. Setting a Session Variable**  
```php
<?php
session_start();
$_SESSION["user_id"] = 101;
$_SESSION["email"] = "user@example.com";
?>
```

### ‚úÖ **2. Retrieving a Session Variable**  
```php
<?php
session_start();
echo "User ID: " . $_SESSION["user_id"] . "<br>";
echo "Email: " . $_SESSION["email"];
?>
```

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Destroying a Session**  

üîπ **Session ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:**  
1. **Session Variables Unset ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®** ‚Üí `session_unset()`  
2. **Session Destroy ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®** ‚Üí `session_destroy()`  
3. **Session Cookie ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®** ‚Üí `setcookie(session_name(), "", time() - 3600, "/")`  

‚úÖ **Example: Destroy a Session**  
```php
<?php
session_start();
session_unset();  // Remove all session variables
session_destroy(); // Destroy the session
setcookie(session_name(), "", time() - 3600, "/"); // Delete session cookie
echo "Session Destroyed!";
?>
```

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Session Timeout and Auto Expiry**  

üîπ **Session timeout ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `$_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY']` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Auto Logout After 10 Minutes**  
```php
<?php
session_start();

if (isset($_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY']) && (time() - $_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY'] > 600)) { // 600 seconds = 10 minutes
    session_unset();
    session_destroy();
    echo "Session expired due to inactivity.";
} else {
    $_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY'] = time(); // Update last activity timestamp
}
?>
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **User 10 ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø inactive ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá session destroy ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Session Security Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **1. Use `session_regenerate_id()` to Prevent Session Hijacking**  
```php
session_start();
session_regenerate_id(true); // Change session ID to prevent hijacking
```

‚úÖ **2. Use `session_set_cookie_params()` for Secure Cookies**  
```php
session_set_cookie_params([
    'lifetime' => 0,
    'path' => '/',
    'domain' => '',
    'secure' => true,   // Only send over HTTPS
    'httponly' => true, // Prevent JavaScript access
    'samesite' => 'Strict'
]);
session_start();
```

‚úÖ **3. Store Session Data in a Secure Directory**  
```php
session_save_path("/secure_sessions/");
session_start();
```

‚úÖ **4. Prevent Session Fixation**  
```php
session_start();
session_regenerate_id(true);
```

‚úÖ **5. Destroy Session After Logout**  
```php
session_start();
session_unset();
session_destroy();
setcookie(session_name(), "", time() - 3600, "/");
```

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **Use `session_start()` at the Beginning of the Script**  
```php
session_start();
```

‚úÖ **Always Unset and Destroy Session on Logout**  
```php
session_unset();
session_destroy();
```

‚úÖ **Use Secure Cookie Parameters**  
```php
session_set_cookie_params(['secure' => true, 'httponly' => true]);
```

‚úÖ **Set Session Timeout to Prevent Unauthorized Access**  
```php
$_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY'] = time();
if (time() - $_SESSION['LAST_ACTIVITY'] > 600) { session_destroy(); }
```

‚úÖ **Store Sensitive Data Securely**  
```php
$_SESSION["user_data"] = password_hash("secureData", PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **Sessions** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **user data store ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç multiple page-‡¶è persist** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **authentication, shopping cart, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user preferences management** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§  

üîπ **Key Features:**  
- **Server-side data storage** (Cookies ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã client-side ‡¶®‡ßü)‡•§  
- **Security ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø** ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ data **server-‡¶è store ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§  
- **Session Timeout ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Expiry ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**‡•§  
- **Session Hijacking ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ö‡¶§‡ßá `session_regenerate_id()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§**

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-27: PHP Filters

PHP **Filters** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü **user input validation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data sanitization** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **user-submitted data clean, validate ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What are PHP Filters?**  

‚úÖ **PHP Filters** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **built-in functions**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **data sanitize ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§  
‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **malicious input ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç security vulnerabilities (SQL Injection, XSS, etc.) ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  

‚úÖ **Common Use Cases:**  
- **User-submitted form data clean ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§**  
- **SQL Injection ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç XSS ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§**  
- **Integer, Float, Email, URL ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§**  

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use PHP Filters?**  

üîπ **Security:** Malicious input ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
üîπ **Data Integrity:** Database-‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ valid data save ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
üîπ **Error Handling:** Input validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá error management ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
üîπ **Code Efficiency:** Built-in functions ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá input validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **PHP Filter Functions**  

PHP ‡¶§‡ßá **filtering ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç validation** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:  

| Function | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `filter_var()` | Single value sanitize ‡¶¨‡¶æ validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |
| `filter_input()` | `$_GET`, `$_POST`, `$_COOKIE`, `$_SERVER` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø data filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |
| `filter_input_array()` | ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï input filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Validating Data with `filter_var()`**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá `filter_var()` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á data validation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Validate an Email Address**  
```php
<?php
$email = "test@example.com";
if (filter_var($email, FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {
    echo "Valid Email";
} else {
    echo "Invalid Email";
}
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Validate an Integer**  
```php
<?php
$age = "25";
if (filter_var($age, FILTER_VALIDATE_INT)) {
    echo "Valid Integer";
} else {
    echo "Invalid Integer";
}
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Validate a URL**  
```php
<?php
$url = "https://www.example.com";
if (filter_var($url, FILTER_VALIDATE_URL)) {
    echo "Valid URL";
} else {
    echo "Invalid URL";
}
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Validate an IP Address**  
```php
<?php
$ip = "192.168.1.1";
if (filter_var($ip, FILTER_VALIDATE_IP)) {
    echo "Valid IP Address";
} else {
    echo "Invalid IP Address";
}
?>
```

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Sanitizing Data with `filter_var()`**  

üîπ **Sanitization ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü user input ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá unwanted characters remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Sanitize an Email Address**  
```php
<?php
$email = "test@@example.com";
$clean_email = filter_var($email, FILTER_SANITIZE_EMAIL);
echo $clean_email; // Output: test@example.com
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Sanitize a String (Remove Special Characters)**  
```php
<?php
$string = "<h1>Hello World!</h1>";
$clean_string = filter_var($string, FILTER_SANITIZE_STRING);
echo $clean_string; // Output: Hello World!
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Sanitize a URL**  
```php
<?php
$url = "https://www.example.com?name=<script>alert('XSS')</script>";
$clean_url = filter_var($url, FILTER_SANITIZE_URL);
echo $clean_url;
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Sanitize an Integer**  
```php
<?php
$number = "45abc";
$clean_number = filter_var($number, FILTER_SANITIZE_NUMBER_INT);
echo $clean_number; // Output: 45
?>
```

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Using `filter_input()` for Form Data**  

üîπ **`filter_input()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü form data ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø input validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Validate Email from `$_POST` Form**  
```php
<?php
if ($_SERVER["REQUEST_METHOD"] == "POST") {
    $email = filter_input(INPUT_POST, "email", FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL);
    if ($email) {
        echo "Valid Email";
    } else {
        echo "Invalid Email";
    }
}
?>
<form method="post">
    <input type="email" name="email">
    <input type="submit">
</form>
```

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Using `filter_input_array()` for Multiple Inputs**  

‚úÖ **Example: Validate Multiple Inputs from `$_POST` Form**  
```php
<?php
if ($_SERVER["REQUEST_METHOD"] == "POST") {
    $filters = [
        "email" => FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL,
        "age" => FILTER_VALIDATE_INT
    ];
    
    $input = filter_input_array(INPUT_POST, $filters);

    if ($input["email"] && $input["age"]) {
        echo "Valid Inputs";
    } else {
        echo "Invalid Inputs";
    }
}
?>
<form method="post">
    Email: <input type="email" name="email"><br>
    Age: <input type="text" name="age"><br>
    <input type="submit">
</form>
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Multiple fields validate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `filter_input_array()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Custom Validation with Filters**  

‚úÖ **Example: Validate a String with a Custom Regular Expression**  
```php
<?php
function validate_username($username) {
    return preg_match("/^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{5,20}$/", $username);
}

$username = "User_123";
if (validate_username($username)) {
    echo "Valid Username";
} else {
    echo "Invalid Username";
}
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Username ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ alphanumeric characters ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç underscores ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 9Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **Always Validate and Sanitize User Input**  
```php
$email = filter_var($_POST["email"], FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL);
```

‚úÖ **Use `filter_input()` Instead of Direct Access to `$_POST` or `$_GET`**  
```php
$name = filter_input(INPUT_POST, "name", FILTER_SANITIZE_STRING);
```

‚úÖ **Use `filter_var()` for Cleaning Data Before Saving to Database**  
```php
$clean_data = filter_var($data, FILTER_SANITIZE_STRING);
```

‚úÖ **Use `filter_input_array()` for Handling Multiple Fields at Once**  
```php
$input = filter_input_array(INPUT_POST, $filters);
```

‚úÖ **Always Use `FILTER_VALIDATE_*` Instead of Custom Regex When Possible**  
```php
if (filter_var($email, FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL)) {
    echo "Valid Email!";
}
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **Filters** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **user input validation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç sanitization** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **security vulnerabilities ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  

üîπ **Key Functions:**  
- `filter_var()` ‚Üí Data validate ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç sanitize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  
- `filter_input()` ‚Üí Form input ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  
- `filter_input_array()` ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï input filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  

<div align="right">
    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-28: PHP Callback Functions

PHP **Callback Functions** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **functions ‡¶Ø‡¶æ argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø function ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá **execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **functional programming, array processing, event handling, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç asynchronous execution** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  

---

## **Table of Contents**
1. [What is a PHP Callback Function?](#what-is-a-php-callback-function)  
2. [Why Use Callback Functions?](#why-use-callback-functions)  
3. [Simple Callback Function](#simple-callback-function)  
4. [Using Anonymous Functions as Callbacks](#using-anonymous-functions-as-callbacks)  
5. [Using PHP Built-in Callback Functions](#using-php-built-in-callback-functions)  
6. [Callback with `call_user_func()` and `call_user_func_array()`](#callback-with-call_user_func-and-call_user_func_array)  
7. [Using Callback Functions with Classes](#using-callback-functions-with-classes)  
8. [Best Practices](#best-practices)  

---

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What is a PHP Callback Function?**  

‚úÖ **PHP Callback Function** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø function ‡¶è‡¶∞ argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§  
‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **higher-order functions** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **functional programming** ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  

‚úÖ **Use Cases:**  
- **Custom Sorting Algorithms** (`usort()`)  
- **Array Processing** (`array_map()`, `array_filter()`)  
- **Event Handling & Hooks**  
- **Asynchronous Execution**  

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use Callback Functions?**  

üîπ **Code Reusability:** Dynamic logic pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  
üîπ **Higher-Order Function Support:** Functions **flexible** ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
üîπ **Asynchronous Processing Possible:** Delayed execution ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
üîπ **Event Handling:** Hooks & listeners ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **Simple Callback Function**  

‚úÖ **Example: Callback Function Passing**  
```php
<?php
function greet($name) {
    echo "Hello, $name!";
}

function processUser($callback, $name) {
    $callback($name);
}

processUser("greet", "John"); // Output: Hello, John!
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
1. `greet()` function user ‡¶ï‡ßá greet ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
2. `processUser()` function ‡¶è **callback function ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç name pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá**‡•§  
3. `$callback($name)` ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **callback function execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá**‡•§  

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Using Anonymous Functions as Callbacks**  

‚úÖ **Example: Passing an Anonymous Function as a Callback**  
```php
<?php
function process($callback) {
    $callback();
}

process(function() {
    echo "Anonymous function executed!";
});
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Anonymous Function** callback ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  
- **Direct function call ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, dynamic execution ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Using PHP Built-in Callback Functions**  

üîπ PHP ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï **built-in functions** ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ callback ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  

‚úÖ **Example: Using `array_map()` for Transformation**  
```php
<?php
$numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

$squared = array_map(function($n) {
    return $n * $n;
}, $numbers);

print_r($squared); // Output: [1, 4, 9, 16, 25]
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Using `array_filter()` for Filtering**  
```php
<?php
$numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];

$evenNumbers = array_filter($numbers, function($n) {
    return $n % 2 === 0;
});

print_r($evenNumbers); // Output: [2, 4]
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Using `usort()` for Custom Sorting**  
```php
<?php
$names = ["Alice", "Bob", "Charlie", "Dave"];

usort($names, function($a, $b) {
    return strlen($a) - strlen($b); // Sort by string length
});

print_r($names);
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`array_map()` ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  
- **`array_filter()` ‚Üí ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ elements filter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  
- **`usort()` ‚Üí Custom sorting logic apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Callback with `call_user_func()` and `call_user_func_array()`**  

üîπ **`call_user_func()`** ‚Üí Callback function **dynamically call** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
üîπ **`call_user_func_array()`** ‚Üí Callback function ‡¶ï‡ßá **array of arguments** ‡¶∏‡¶π call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  

‚úÖ **Example: Using `call_user_func()`**  
```php
<?php
function greet($name) {
    return "Hello, $name!";
}

echo call_user_func("greet", "John"); // Output: Hello, John!
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Using `call_user_func_array()` with Multiple Arguments**  
```php
<?php
function add($a, $b) {
    return $a + $b;
}

echo call_user_func_array("add", [5, 10]); // Output: 15
?>
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`call_user_func()` ‚Üí Callback function ‡¶ï‡ßá dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  
- **`call_user_func_array()` ‚Üí Arguments list array ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá function call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Using Callback Functions with Classes**  

‚úÖ **Example: Using Object Methods as Callbacks**  
```php
<?php
class Greeting {
    public function sayHello($name) {
        return "Hello, $name!";
    }
}

$obj = new Greeting();
echo call_user_func([$obj, "sayHello"], "John"); // Output: Hello, John!
?>
```

‚úÖ **Example: Using Static Method as Callback**  
```php
<?php
class Math {
    public static function square($n) {
        return $n * $n;
    }
}

$numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];
$squared = array_map(["Math", "square"], $numbers);

print_r($squared); // Output: [1, 4, 9, 16, 25]
?>
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Object Methods Callback ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  
- **Static Methods Callback ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `array_map()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **Use Anonymous Functions for Small Callbacks**  
```php
array_map(fn($n) => $n * 2, $numbers);
```

‚úÖ **Use Named Functions for Reusability**  
```php
function square($n) { return $n * $n; }
array_map("square", $numbers);
```

‚úÖ **Use `call_user_func()` for Dynamic Function Calls**  
```php
call_user_func("greet", "John");
```

‚úÖ **Use `call_user_func_array()` for Variable Arguments**  
```php
call_user_func_array("add", [10, 20]);
```

‚úÖ **Use Classes for Clean Code**  
```php
call_user_func(["Math", "square"], 5);
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **Callback Functions** **higher-order function support, asynchronous execution, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç custom logic pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  

üîπ **Key Features:**  
- `functionName` ‚Üí Function name callback ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  
- `anonymous function` ‚Üí Dynamic execution ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- `call_user_func()` ‚Üí Dynamic function calls ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  
- `array_map()`, `array_filter()`, `usort()` ‚Üí Built-in callback support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- `Classes & Methods` ‚Üí Callback ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  

<div align="right">
    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-29: PHP and JSON

PHP **JSON (JavaScript Object Notation)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **lightweight data exchange format**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **PHP ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø programming language-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º**‡•§  

---

## **Table of Contents**
1. [What is JSON?](#what-is-json)  
2. [Why Use JSON in PHP?](#why-use-json-in-php)  
3. [Converting PHP Data to JSON (`json_encode()`)](#converting-php-data-to-json-json_encode)  
4. [Converting JSON to PHP (`json_decode()`)](#converting-json-to-php-json_decode)  
5. [Working with Associative Arrays and Objects](#working-with-associative-arrays-and-objects)  
6. [Handling JSON Errors](#handling-json-errors)  
7. [Reading and Writing JSON Files in PHP](#reading-and-writing-json-files-in-php)  
8. [Best Practices](#best-practices)  

---

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What is JSON?**  

‚úÖ **JSON (JavaScript Object Notation)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **human-readable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç machine-readable data format**‡•§  
‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **key-value pairs** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  

‚úÖ **Example JSON Data:**  
```json
{
    "name": "John Doe",
    "age": 30,
    "email": "john@example.com",
    "skills": ["PHP", "JavaScript", "Python"]
}
```

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use JSON in PHP?**  

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **Lightweight Format** | XML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º **‡¶ï‡¶Æ resource consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§ |
| **Human & Machine Readable** | ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç parse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |
| **API Communication** | REST API ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç AJAX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **client-server data exchange** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |
| **Cross-Platform Support** | JSON **PHP, JavaScript, Python, Java, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§**‡•§ |

‚úÖ **Common Use Cases:**  
- **API Response Formatting**  
- **AJAX Requests Handling**  
- **Database Query Results Encoding**  
- **Configuration Files**  

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **Converting PHP Data to JSON (`json_encode()`)**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá `json_encode()` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá JSON format ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Convert PHP Array to JSON**  
```php
<?php
$data = [
    "name" => "John Doe",
    "age" => 30,
    "email" => "john@example.com",
    "skills" => ["PHP", "JavaScript", "Python"]
];

$json_data = json_encode($data, JSON_PRETTY_PRINT);
echo $json_data;
?>
```
üîπ **Output (Formatted JSON):**  
```json
{
    "name": "John Doe",
    "age": 30,
    "email": "john@example.com",
    "skills": ["PHP", "JavaScript", "Python"]
}
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- `json_encode($data)` ‚Üí PHP array ‡¶ï‡ßá JSON string ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- `JSON_PRETTY_PRINT` ‚Üí JSON output ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá format ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Converting JSON to PHP (`json_decode()`)**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá `json_decode()` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá JSON ‡¶ï‡ßá PHP array ‡¶¨‡¶æ object ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Convert JSON to PHP Array**  
```php
<?php
$json = '{"name":"John Doe","age":30,"email":"john@example.com","skills":["PHP","JavaScript","Python"]}';

$data = json_decode($json, true); // Convert JSON to associative array

echo "Name: " . $data["name"];
echo "Email: " . $data["email"];
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
Name: John Doe
Email: john@example.com
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- `json_decode($json, true)` ‚Üí JSON ‡¶ï‡ßá PHP **Associative Array** ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- `json_decode($json)` ‚Üí **PHP Object** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (default)‡•§  

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Working with Associative Arrays and Objects**  

üîπ **PHP Object ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `json_decode()` ‡¶è `false` pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Convert JSON to PHP Object**  
```php
<?php
$json = '{"name":"John Doe","age":30,"email":"john@example.com"}';

$data = json_decode($json); // Convert to PHP Object

echo "Name: " . $data->name;
echo "Email: " . $data->email;
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
Name: John Doe
Email: john@example.com
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Object Notation:** `$data->name`  
- **Associative Array Notation:** `$data["name"]`  

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Handling JSON Errors**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá JSON error check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `json_last_error()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `json_last_error_msg()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Error Handling in JSON Parsing**  
```php
<?php
$json = '{"name":"John Doe","age":30,}'; // Invalid JSON (extra comma)

$data = json_decode($json);

if (json_last_error() !== JSON_ERROR_NONE) {
    echo "JSON Error: " . json_last_error_msg();
} else {
    echo "Name: " . $data->name;
}
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
JSON Error: Syntax error
```

‚úÖ **Common JSON Errors:**  

| Error Code | Description |
|------------|-------------|
| `JSON_ERROR_NONE` | No error |
| `JSON_ERROR_SYNTAX` | Syntax error in JSON |
| `JSON_ERROR_DEPTH` | Maximum stack depth exceeded |
| `JSON_ERROR_UTF8` | Malformed UTF-8 characters |

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Reading and Writing JSON Files in PHP**  

‚úÖ **Example: Writing JSON Data to a File**  
```php
<?php
$data = [
    "name" => "John Doe",
    "age" => 30,
    "email" => "john@example.com"
];

file_put_contents("data.json", json_encode($data, JSON_PRETTY_PRINT));
echo "JSON file created!";
?>
```
üîπ **Output:** (File: `data.json`)  
```json
{
    "name": "John Doe",
    "age": 30,
    "email": "john@example.com"
}
```

‚úÖ **Example: Reading JSON Data from a File**  
```php
<?php
$json = file_get_contents("data.json");
$data = json_decode($json, true);

echo "Name: " . $data["name"];
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
Name: John Doe
```

‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`file_put_contents()`** ‚Üí JSON data **‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá**‡•§  
- **`file_get_contents()`** ‚Üí JSON data **‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá**‡•§  

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **Always Check for JSON Errors**  
```php
if (json_last_error() !== JSON_ERROR_NONE) {
    echo "Error in JSON: " . json_last_error_msg();
}
```

‚úÖ **Use `JSON_PRETTY_PRINT` for Readable Output**  
```php
json_encode($data, JSON_PRETTY_PRINT);
```

‚úÖ **Use `json_decode($json, true)` to Get an Associative Array**  
```php
$data = json_decode($json, true);
```

‚úÖ **Use `file_get_contents()` and `file_put_contents()` for File Handling**  
```php
$json = file_get_contents("data.json");
$data = json_decode($json, true);
```

‚úÖ **Ensure Valid JSON Format Before Decoding**  
```php
if (!json_decode($json)) {
    die("Invalid JSON format");
}
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **JSON Handling** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **data serialize, store, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç API communication** ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  

üîπ **Key Features:**  
- `json_encode()` ‚Üí **PHP data ‚Üí JSON**  
- `json_decode()` ‚Üí **JSON ‚Üí PHP data**  
- `file_get_contents()` & `file_put_contents()` ‚Üí **JSON file read & write**  
- `json_last_error_msg()` ‚Üí **JSON errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ**

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-30: PHP Exceptions

PHP **Exceptions** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **error handling mechanism**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **unexpected errors gracefully handle** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **try, catch, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç throw** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **custom error messages ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç debugging ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  

---

## **Table of Contents**  
1. [What is an Exception in PHP?](#what-is-an-exception-in-php)  
2. [Why Use Exceptions?](#why-use-exceptions)  
3. [PHP Exception Handling (`try`, `catch`, `throw`)](#php-exception-handling-try-catch-throw)  
4. [Creating Custom Exception Classes](#creating-custom-exception-classes)

8. [Best Practices](#best-practices)  

---

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ **What is an Exception in PHP?**  

‚úÖ **PHP Exception** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **runtime error handling mechanism**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **unexpected errors** handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **try-catch block ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§**  
‚úÖ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **program execution ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá error log ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç custom messages ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§  

üîπ **Example Exceptions:**  
- **Divide by Zero Error**  
- **File Not Found Error**  
- **Database Connection Error**  
- **Invalid Input Handling**  

---

## 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Why Use Exceptions?**  

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **Error Handling** | Unexpected errors handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| **Code Maintainability** | `try-catch` block ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá code cleaner ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |
| **Prevents Fatal Errors** | Program crash ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá error message return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ |
| **Improves Debugging** | Custom error messages ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logging ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |

---

## 3Ô∏è‚É£ **PHP Exception Handling (`try`, `catch`, `throw`)**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá `try-catch` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Exception handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  
üîπ **`throw` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá custom Exception trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Basic Exception Handling**  
```php
<?php
try {
    // Code that may cause an exception
    if (rand(1, 10) > 5) {
        throw new Exception("Random Exception Triggered!");
    }
    echo "No Exception Occurred!";
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Error: " . $e->getMessage();
}
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`try {}` block** ‚Üí ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **error-prone code** ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- **`throw new Exception("message")`** ‚Üí Custom error throw ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
- **`catch (Exception $e) {}`** ‚Üí Exception handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç message display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  

---

## 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Creating Custom Exception Classes**  

üîπ **PHP ‡¶§‡ßá Custom Exception ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `Exception` class extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Custom Exception Class**  
```php
<?php
class MyException extends Exception {
    public function errorMessage() {
        return "Custom Error: " . $this->getMessage();
    }
}

try {
    throw new MyException("Something went wrong!");
} catch (MyException $e) {
    echo $e->errorMessage();
}
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Custom Exception Class ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  
- **Custom error message return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Using Multiple `catch` Blocks**  

üîπ **Different Exceptions handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø multiple `catch` blocks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Handling Multiple Exceptions**  
```php
<?php
try {
    $x = rand(1, 3);
    if ($x == 1) {
        throw new Exception("General Exception!");
    } elseif ($x == 2) {
        throw new InvalidArgumentException("Invalid Argument Exception!");
    }
} catch (InvalidArgumentException $e) {
    echo "Caught: " . $e->getMessage();
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Caught General Exception: " . $e->getMessage();
}
?>
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **Different types of exceptions handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  
- **Specific exception (`InvalidArgumentException`) ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá catch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 6Ô∏è‚É£ **Using `finally` for Cleanup Code**  

üîπ **`finally` block ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü execute ‡¶π‡ßü, exception ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Using `finally` for Cleanup**  
```php
<?php
try {
    throw new Exception("An error occurred!");
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Caught Exception: " . $e->getMessage();
} finally {
    echo " - Cleanup process completed!";
}
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
Caught Exception: An error occurred! - Cleanup process completed!
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`finally` block ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü execute ‡¶π‡ßü, resource cleanup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§**  

---

## 7Ô∏è‚É£ **Exception Handling in Functions**  

üîπ **Functions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá `throw` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá exception trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§**  

‚úÖ **Example: Handling Exception in Function**  
```php
<?php
function divide($a, $b) {
    if ($b == 0) {
        throw new Exception("Division by zero not allowed!");
    }
    return $a / $b;
}

try {
    echo divide(10, 0);
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Error: " . $e->getMessage();
}
?>
```
üîπ **Output:**  
```
Error: Division by zero not allowed!
```
‚úÖ **Explanation:**  
- **`throw` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá function ‡¶è error handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§**  

---

## 8Ô∏è‚É£ **Best Practices**  

‚úÖ **1. Always Use `try-catch` for Critical Code**  
```php
try {
    // Critical operations
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Error: " . $e->getMessage();
}
```

‚úÖ **2. Use `finally` for Resource Cleanup**  
```php
try {
    // Database connection
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Error: " . $e->getMessage();
} finally {
    // Close database connection
}
```

‚úÖ **3. Create Custom Exception Classes for Better Organization**  
```php
class DatabaseException extends Exception {
    public function errorMessage() {
        return "Database Error: " . $this->getMessage();
    }
}
```

‚úÖ **4. Log Exceptions for Debugging**  
```php
try {
    throw new Exception("Fatal Error!");
} catch (Exception $e) {
    error_log($e->getMessage(), 3, "errors.log");
}
```

‚úÖ **5. Use `set_exception_handler()` for Global Exception Handling**  
```php
function exceptionHandler($exception) {
    echo "Uncaught Exception: " . $exception->getMessage();
}

set_exception_handler("exceptionHandler");

throw new Exception("Something went wrong!");
```

---

## üéØ **Final Summary**  

PHP **Exceptions** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **error handling process efficient, secure, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  

üîπ **Key Features:**  
- `try-catch` ‚Üí Exception handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- `throw` ‚Üí Custom exceptions trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- `finally` ‚Üí Cleanup operations manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- `Custom Exception Classes` ‚Üí Specific error types handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- `set_exception_handler()` ‚Üí Global exception handling ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>

## 1. Introduction to OOP in PHP

PHP traditionally ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤ procedural, ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶ü‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø system-‡¶è‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá:

- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‚úÖ  
- ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‚úÖ  
- ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü ‚úÖ  

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá **Object-Oriented Programming (OOP)**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ PHP-‡¶§‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§

PHP OOP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤:  
1Ô∏è‚É£ **Class & Object** ‚Äì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Object ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã  
2Ô∏è‚É£ **Encapsulation** ‚Äì Data ‡¶ó‡ßã‡¶™‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ  
3Ô∏è‚É£ **Inheritance** ‚Äì ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Class ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ  
4Ô∏è‚É£ **Polymorphism** ‚Äì ‡¶è‡¶ï Method ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Class-‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá  

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡•§

---

## 2. The Story: The World of "SmartFarm" üåæ

‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶á ‚Äî **SmartFarm**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§  

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® **Animal** ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ó‡¶∞‡ßÅ, ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ó‡¶ø, ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡•§  
- ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â **sound** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â **milk** ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§  
- ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ **‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá organize** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ!  
- ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ **behave** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§  

‡¶è‡¶á Farm-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßã PHP OOP!

---

## 3. Class and Object

### üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
Class ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ**, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Object-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú (Method) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Object ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ‡•§

### üí° ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
SmartFarm-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‚Äî ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá Class‡•§

```php
<?php
class Animal {
    public $name;
    public $type;

    public function __construct($name, $type) {
        $this->name = $name;
        $this->type = $type;
    }

    public function introduce() {
        echo "I am $this->name and I am a $this->type.<br>";
    }
}

$cow = new Animal("Mala", "Cow");
$goat = new Animal("Buli", "Goat");

$cow->introduce();
$goat->introduce();
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Animal` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Class ‚Äî ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ `Mala` ‡¶ì `Buli` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Object‡•§

---

## 4. Encapsulation ‚Äì Keeping Things Safe

### üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
Encapsulation ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **Data Hide** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá `private` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ Access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `public` Method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

### üí° ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶ó‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ß ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø **private** ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§

```php
<?php
class Cow {
    private $milkAmount;

    public function __construct($milk) {
        $this->milkAmount = $milk;
    }

    public function addMilk($amount) {
        $this->milkAmount += $amount;
    }

    public function getMilk() {
        return $this->milkAmount . " liters of milk<br>";
    }
}

$mala = new Cow(5);
$mala->addMilk(3);
echo $mala->getMilk(); // 8 liters of milk
?>
```

üìå `milkAmount`-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ Method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 5. Inheritance ‚Äì Passing Down the Features

### üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
Inheritance ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Class-‡¶è **Reuse** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶É‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### üí° ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
Animal Class ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Cow Class ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `Animal` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
class Animal {
    public $name;

    public function __construct($name) {
        $this->name = $name;
    }

    public function makeSound() {
        echo "$this->name makes a sound.<br>";
    }
}

class Cow extends Animal {
    public function makeSound() {
        echo "$this->name says Hamba!<br>";
    }
}

$mala = new Cow("Mala");
$mala->makeSound();
?>
```

üìå `Cow` ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ `Animal`-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶° ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã `makeSound()` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 6. Polymorphism ‚Äì One Interface, Many Behaviors

### üéØ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
Polymorphism ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ Method, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Class-‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£‡•§

### üí° ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:
‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `makeSound()` ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶•‡¶° ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï Array-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶£‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
class Goat extends Animal {
    public function makeSound() {
        echo "$this->name says Baaaa!<br>";
    }
}

$animals = [
    new Cow("Mala"),
    new Goat("Buli")
];

foreach ($animals as $animal) {
    $animal->makeSound();
}
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á `makeSound()` ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Class ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ output ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 7. Real-life Example: Building a Simple Product System

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü E-Commerce ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Product ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
class Product {
    protected $name;
    protected $price;

    public function __construct($name, $price) {
        $this->name = $name;
        $this->price = $price;
    }

    public function display() {
        echo "Product: $this->name | Price: $this->price<br>";
    }
}

class Book extends Product {
    public function display() {
        echo "üìö Book: $this->name | Price: $this->price<br>";
    }
}

class Laptop extends Product {
    public function display() {
        echo "üíª Laptop: $this->name | Price: $this->price<br>";
    }
}

$items = [
    new Book("PHP Mastery", 25),
    new Laptop("MacBook Air", 999)
];

foreach ($items as $item) {
    $item->display();
}
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Book` ‡¶ì `Laptop` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶á `Product` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

## 1. What are Access Modifiers?

**Access Modifiers** PHP OOP-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Property ‡¶¨‡¶æ Method ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Access Modifiers ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Modifier    | Accessible From |  
|-------------|------------------|  
| `public`    | ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá (class, object, subclass, ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü)  
| `private`   | ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá  
| `protected` | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßá extends ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (subclass)

Access Modifiers ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Code-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßã‡¶™‡¶®‡ßÄ‡ßü‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‚úÖ

---

## 2. Story: The Secret Vault of CodeBank üîí

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® Security Engineer ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® **CodeBank** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá üè¶

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. üëã **General Info**: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ, ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‚Äî ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (public)  
2. üîê **Vault Access Code**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßã‡¶™‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°, ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá (private)  
3. ü§ù **Employee Access Level**: ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßÄ ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá (protected)

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® PHP OOP-‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø Access Modifier ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã ‚Äî ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø!

---

## 3. `public` Modifier

### üîì ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
`public` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Default Access Level‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá (class, object, ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü) property ‡¶¨‡¶æ method access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

### ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
class CodeBank {
    public $bankName = "CodeBank International";

    public function showBankName() {
        echo "Welcome to $this->bankName!<br>";
    }
}

$bank = new CodeBank();
$bank->showBankName();         // Welcome to CodeBank International!
echo $bank->bankName . "<br>"; // Direct access possible
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `bankName` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `showBankName()` ‡¶â‡¶≠‡ßü‡¶á `public`, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á Access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 4. `private` Modifier

### üîí ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
`private` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á property ‡¶¨‡¶æ method ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á class-‡¶è‡¶∞ **‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á** access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶¨‡¶æ subclass ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
class CodeBank {
    private $vaultCode = "XYZ123";

    public function getVaultCode() {
        return "Access Code: $this->vaultCode";
    }
}

$bank = new CodeBank();
// echo $bank->vaultCode; ‚ùå Error: Cannot access private property
echo $bank->getVaultCode();    // ‚úÖ Output: Access Code: XYZ123
?>
```

üìå `vaultCode` ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá error ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ internal method ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## 5. `protected` Modifier

### üõ°Ô∏è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ:
`protected` property ‡¶¨‡¶æ method ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á class ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ subclass ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ code ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### ‚úÖ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
class CodeBank {
    protected $employeeLevel = "Manager";
}

class Employee extends CodeBank {
    public function showLevel() {
        echo "Access Level: $this->employeeLevel<br>";
    }
}

$emp = new Employee();
$emp->showLevel();        // ‚úÖ Accessed via subclass method
// echo $emp->employeeLevel; ‚ùå Error: Cannot access protected property
?>
```

üìå `employeeLevel` ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ object ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ subclass ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## 6. Access Modifiers Comparison Table

| Feature                              | public | private | protected |
|--------------------------------------|--------|---------|-----------|
| Access from inside same class        | ‚úÖ     | ‚úÖ      | ‚úÖ        |
| Access from outside the class        | ‚úÖ     | ‚ùå      | ‚ùå        |
| Access from inherited (child) class  | ‚úÖ     | ‚ùå      | ‚úÖ        |

---

## 7. Real-life Example: Hospital Management System

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Hospital Management System** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

- **public**: ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ  
- **private**: ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü (‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá)  
- **protected**: ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá)

```php
<?php
class Patient {
    public $hospital = "City Hospital";
    private $report = "Confidential";
    protected $doctorNote = "Needs surgery";

    public function getReport() {
        return "Medical Report: $this->report<br>";
    }
}

class Doctor extends Patient {
    public function getDoctorNote() {
        return "Doctor's Note: $this->doctorNote<br>";
    }
}

$patient = new Doctor();

echo $patient->hospital . "<br>";         // ‚úÖ public
echo $patient->getReport();               // ‚úÖ private accessed via method
echo $patient->getDoctorNote();           // ‚úÖ protected accessed via subclass

// echo $patient->report; // ‚ùå Error
// echo $patient->doctorNote; // ‚ùå Error
?>
```

üìå Access Modifier ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ì ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§

## 1. What is Inheritance in PHP OOP?

**Inheritance** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã PHP OOP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful concept ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Class-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ **(properties & methods)** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§

üëâ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Parent/Base Class** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Child Class-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§  
üëâ Child Class ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ method ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Inheritance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `extends` keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**

---

## 2. Story: The Royal Family of CodeKingdom üëë

‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶á **CodeKingdom** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ (King) ‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá (Prince) ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

- ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
- ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  
- ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á Inheritance! ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶æ (Parent Class) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá (Child Class) ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. Basic Inheritance Example

```php
<?php
class King {
    public $name = "King Arthur";

    public function rule() {
        echo "$this->name is ruling the kingdom.<br>";
    }
}

class Prince extends King {
    public function train() {
        echo "Prince is training to rule the kingdom.<br>";
    }
}

$prince = new Prince();
$prince->rule();   // Inherited from King
$prince->train();  // Own method
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Prince` class, `King` class ‡¶ï‡ßá `extends` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá `rule()` method ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `name` property ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 4. Method Overriding

**Child Class ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Parent-‡¶è‡¶∞ method ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá Method Overriding.**

```php
<?php
class King {
    public function rule() {
        echo "King rules with wisdom.<br>";
    }
}

class Prince extends King {
    public function rule() {
        echo "Prince rules with innovation!<br>";
    }
}

$p = new Prince();
$p->rule(); // Output: Prince rules with innovation!
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ method `rule()` ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì Prince ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## 5. Accessing Parent Class from Child using `parent::`

Child class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Parent-‡¶è‡¶∞ overridden method call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `parent::` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
class King {
    public function rule() {
        echo "King rules the old way.<br>";
    }
}

class Prince extends King {
    public function rule() {
        echo "Prince is ruling now...<br>";
        parent::rule(); // Calling parent class method
    }
}

$p = new Prince();
$p->rule();
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Prince-‡¶è‡¶∞ rule() ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ `parent::rule()` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá King's rule() ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## 6. Using Constructor in Inherited Class

Inheritance-‡¶è Constructor ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Parent class-‡¶è‡¶∞ Constructor ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ unless ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø `parent::__construct()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

```php
<?php
class King {
    public function __construct() {
        echo "King is born!<br>";
    }
}

class Prince extends King {
    public function __construct() {
        echo "Prince is born!<br>";
        parent::__construct(); // Calling parent constructor
    }
}

$p = new Prince(); 
?>
```

üìå Prince ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Constructor ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ parent-‡¶è‡¶∞ Constructor ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## 7. Real-life Example: School Management System

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø School Management ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

- `Person` ‚Üí Common Base Class  
- `Student`, `Teacher` ‚Üí Inherited Classes

```php
<?php
class Person {
    public $name;
    public $age;

    public function __construct($name, $age) {
        $this->name = $name;
        $this->age = $age;
    }

    public function introduce() {
        echo "Name: $this->name, Age: $this->age<br>";
    }
}

class Student extends Person {
    public $grade;

    public function __construct($name, $age, $grade) {
        parent::__construct($name, $age);
        $this->grade = $grade;
    }

    public function introduce() {
        parent::introduce();
        echo "Grade: $this->grade<br>";
    }
}

class Teacher extends Person {
    public $subject;

    public function __construct($name, $age, $subject) {
        parent::__construct($name, $age);
        $this->subject = $subject;
    }

    public function introduce() {
        parent::introduce();
        echo "Subject: $this->subject<br>";
    }
}

$student = new Student("Amina", 15, "10");
$teacher = new Teacher("Mr. Karim", 40, "Math");

$student->introduce();
$teacher->introduce();
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á Parent `Person` Class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `Student` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Teacher` ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Property ‡¶ì Method ‡¶™‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ì ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

## 1. What is an Abstract Class in PHP?

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Abstract Class** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Class ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá Object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äì **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø common blueprint** ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßã ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Class ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

üß± Key Points:
- `abstract` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü  
- Abstract class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **Abstract Methods** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá  
- Abstract Method-‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ **body (‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°)** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ declaration ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá  
- ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á class abstract class ‡¶ï‡ßá `extends` ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ abstract method implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá

```php
abstract class Animal {
    abstract public function makeSound();
}
```

üß† ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á Class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Object ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ ‚Äî Object ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ responsibility ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá child class-‡¶è‡¶∞‡•§

---

## 2. Story: The Blueprint of FutureVehicles Inc. üöó

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® Lead Engineer ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® **FutureVehicles Inc.** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶®:

> "‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶á Engine start ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü, Brake ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Abstract Blueprint ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≤ Follow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§"

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Abstract Class `Vehicle` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `Car`, `Bike`, `Truck` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. Creating an Abstract Class

```php
<?php
abstract class Vehicle {
    public $brand;

    public function __construct($brand) {
        $this->brand = $brand;
    }

    // Abstract Method (no body)
    abstract public function startEngine();

    // Concrete Method (with body)
    public function stopEngine() {
        echo "$this->brand engine stopped.<br>";
    }
}
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Vehicle` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Abstract Class  
üìå `startEngine()` method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã body ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø child class ‡¶è define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá  
üìå `stopEngine()` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø regular method, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ child class ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá

---

## 4. Implementing Abstract Methods

```php
<?php
class Car extends Vehicle {
    public function startEngine() {
        echo "$this->brand car engine started with a key!<br>";
    }
}

class Bike extends Vehicle {
    public function startEngine() {
        echo "$this->brand bike engine started with a kick!<br>";
    }
}

$car = new Car("Toyota");
$bike = new Bike("Yamaha");

$car->startEngine();    // Toyota car engine started with a key!
$car->stopEngine();     // Toyota engine stopped.

$bike->startEngine();   // Yamaha bike engine started with a kick!
$bike->stopEngine();    // Yamaha engine stopped.
?>
```

üìå ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Car` ‡¶ì `Bike` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø class `Vehicle` ‡¶ï‡ßá extends ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá  
üìå ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá `startEngine()` define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá  
üìå ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `stopEngine()` use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø parent class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá

---

## 5. Why Abstract Classes?

üëâ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **base class ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï structure ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá**, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® abstract class ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

üß† ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:
- ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÄ sound ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡ßü  
- ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü system process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‚Äî ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá

üü® Interface-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì, Abstract Class-‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø **‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ method define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Interface-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

## 6. Real-life Example: Online Payment System

```php
<?php
abstract class PaymentGateway {
    abstract public function processPayment($amount);

    public function printReceipt($amount) {
        echo "Payment of $$amount processed. Receipt generated.<br>";
    }
}

class Bkash extends PaymentGateway {
    public function processPayment($amount) {
        echo "Processing $$amount via Bkash...<br>";
    }
}

class CreditCard extends PaymentGateway {
    public function processPayment($amount) {
        echo "Processing $$amount via Credit Card...<br>";
    }
}

$payment1 = new Bkash();
$payment1->processPayment(500);
$payment1->printReceipt(500);

$payment2 = new CreditCard();
$payment2->processPayment(1000);
$payment2->printReceipt(1000);
?>
```

üìå `Bkash` ‡¶ì `CreditCard` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø gateway ‡¶á `processPayment()` ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá  
üìå ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ `printReceipt()` method inherited ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá `PaymentGateway` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚¨ÜÔ∏è Go to Top</a></b>
